GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*P**c4/(c5*P + c6)

I need to determine if any candidate formula can match the GT expression:

$$f(P) = 0.9198(1 - P/84.03)P + 0.9198 \cdot P^2/(7.531P + 1)$$

Let me simplify the GT:
$$f(P) = 0.9198P - 0.01095P^2 + 0.9198P^2/(7.531P + 1)$$

This is a function of P only (no t dependence). Let me combine terms over a common denominator:

$$f(P) = \frac{(0.9198P - 0.01095P^2)(7.531P + 1) + 0.9198P^2}{7.531P + 1}$$

Expanding the numerator:
- $0.9198P \cdot 7.531P = 6.927P^2$
- $0.9198P \cdot 1 = 0.9198P$
- $-0.01095P^2 \cdot 7.531P = -0.08246P^3$
- $-0.01095P^2 \cdot 1 = -0.01095P^2$
- $+0.9198P^2$

Total: $-0.08246P^3 + (6.927 - 0.01095 + 0.9198)P^2 + 0.9198P$
$= -0.08246P^3 + 7.836P^2 + 0.9198P$

So: $f(P) = \frac{-0.08246P^3 + 7.836P^2 + 0.9198P}{7.531P + 1}$

This equals: $\frac{c_0 P^3 + c_3 P^2 + c_4 P}{c_1 P + c_2}$

Now let me check **Candidate 9**: $\frac{c_0 P^3}{c_1 P + c_2} + \frac{c_3 P^2}{c_1 P + c_2} + \frac{c_4 P}{c_1 P + c_2}$

This combines to: $\frac{c_0 P^3 + c_3 P^2 + c_4 P}{c_1 P + c_2}$

This is exactly the form I derived! Setting:
- $c_1 = 7.531$ (denominator P coefficient)
- $c_2 = 1$ (denominator constant)
- $c_0 = -0.08246$ (P³ coefficient)
- $c_3 = 7.836$ (P² coefficient)  
- $c_4 = 0.9198$ (P coefficient)

This matches perfectly.

Let me verify: several other candidates might also work. For instance, **Candidate 10** has the same structure as 9 but with an extra $P^2$ term - it would also work (with redundant parameters combining: $c_3 + c_4$ for the $P^2$ coefficient).

Similarly, candidates 3, 8, 18, 29, etc. with the same denominator structure and enough terms would work.

But Candidate 9 is the cleanest exact match.

Let me double-check Candidate 6: $P^3 c_0/(Pc_1+1) + P^2 c_2 + Pc_3$

This equals $\frac{c_0 P^3 + (P c_1+1)(c_2 P^2 + c_3 P)}{Pc_1+1} = \frac{c_0 P^3 + c_1 c_2 P^3 + c_2 P^2 + c_1 c_3 P^2 + c_3 P}{Pc_1+1}$

The numerator is $(c_0 + c_1 c_2)P^3 + (c_2 + c_1 c_3)P^2 + c_3 P$. We need:
- $c_0 + c_1 c_2 = -0.08246$
- $c_2 + c_1 c_3 = 7.836$
- $c_3 = 0.9198$
- $c_1 = 7.531$

From these: $c_3 = 0.9198$, $c_1 = 7.531$, $c_2 = 7.836 - 7.531 \times 0.9198 = 7.836 - 6.927 = 0.909$, $c_0 = -0.08246 - 7.531 \times 0.909 = -0.08246 - 6.844 = -6.927$. This works too!
